She helped me carefully select a room that I liked! I was deeply moved! Thank you for her care and sincerity! In addition, the two small desserts given upon check-in were particularly delicious üòãüòçüòú Thank you very much for a new day, a new place, and a new experience... In the future, I can apply to become a member. I will choose Hilton when I go out in the future! Food, swimming, and fitness are integrated! Good hotel, high quality, happy! Comfortable! Like myself!
The only drawback is that the upgraded 11th floor of the hotel's executive floor actually has no desk lamps, coffee cups, and üç¥equipment for guests to eat on their own. The answer I got after asking is indeed true. According to my experience, these should be standard in all four-star and above hotels! ? It should be improved as appropriate! Also, our flight back to Beijing yesterday was around 5pm. I applied for an extension from the green-clad waiter at the front desk early in the morning, and was told that "it's only until 2pm, you can't stay on time, otherwise you will be charged a half-day accommodation fee." I understand the hotel's regulations very well, but I hope that it will be flexible and increased to 2:30pm according to different people? As a result, my 70-year-old man sat in the lobby for more than an hour yesterday, which was very unpleasant! I deeply felt that entering the store was like a spring breeze, and snacks were given and smiles were given. When leaving the store, "It has nothing to do with me" and "You have money to stay longer." It's none of my business, a cold reception for a cone business? !
But, anyway, I still want to give a thumbs up to this hotel. During the May Day holiday, there were huge crowds of people for breakfast. The hotel staff were dedicated to their duties, especially the two older gentlemen who were managers or supervisors and were very busy. The two cleaners with short hair and ponytails on the 11th floor were also very professional and enthusiastic. I would like to thank them all here!
